***залюбоваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:залюбоваться.html>залюбова́ться</a> (17545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любоваться.html>любова́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubovátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залюбоваться.html>залюбова́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaljubovátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любоваться.html>любова́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stare in an admiring fashion <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, at something/someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***заляпать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заляпать.html>заля́пать</a> (15515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ля́пать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljápatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заляпать.html>заля́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaljápatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заля́пывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slap, to splotch, to daub (paint on something)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ля́пать</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ljápatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ляпнуть.html>ля́пнуть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ljápnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сля́пать</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sljápatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наля́пать</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">naljápatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***замазать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замазать.html>зама́зать</a> (17572)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замазать.html>зама́зать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamázatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замазывать.html>зама́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to paint over</li>
<li>to stick with putty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замазать.html>зама́зать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окна</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зима.html>зи́му</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamázatʹ</b> okna na zímu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seal (up) [stop up] the windows with putty for the winter</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to daub over, to make dirty, to stain</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to efface, to slur over

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замазывавший.html>зама́зывавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamázyvavšij</span>)

***замазывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замазывать.html>зама́зывать</a> (31320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замазать.html>зама́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замазывать.html>зама́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamázyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замазать.html>зама́зать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to paint over</li>
<li>to stick with putty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замазывать.html>зама́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окна</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зима.html>зи́му</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamázyvatʹ</b> okna na zímu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seal (up) [stop up] the windows with putty for the winter</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to daub over, to make dirty, to stain</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to efface, to slur over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замазывать.html>зама́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamázyvatʹ</b> ošíbki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slur over the mistakes</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помазать.html>пома́зать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pomázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вымазать.html>вы́мазать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výmazatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промазать.html>прома́зать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">promázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***заманивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заманивать.html>зама́нивать</a> (18966)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заманить.html>замани́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamanítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заманивать.html>зама́нивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamánivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заманить.html>замани́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заманить.html>замани́ть</a> (12971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манить.html>мани́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">manítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заманить.html>замани́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamanítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заманивать.html>зама́нивать</a></b>)

***замарать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замарать.html>замара́ть</a> (24777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:марать.html>мара́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">marátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замарать.html>замара́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamarátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:марать.html>мара́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зама́рывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to soil, to dirty, to pollute</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to defame, to disgrace</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замаскированный.html>замаскированный</a> (13265)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замаскированный.html>замаскиро́ванный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamaskiróvannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замаскировать.html>замаскирова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamaskirovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замаскированный.html>замаскиро́ванный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamaskiróvannyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)замаскиро́ваннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)замаскиро́ванней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>masked
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замаскированный.html>замаскиро́ванный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужчина.html>мужчи́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamaskiróvannyj</b> mužčína</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>masked</b> man</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>disguised, hidden, secret
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замаскированный.html>замаскиро́ванные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:намерение.html>наме́рения</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamaskiróvannyje</b> namérenija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>disguised</b> intentions</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замаскировать.html>замаскирова́ть</a> (22701)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маскировать.html>маскирова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maskirovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замаскировать.html>замаскирова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamaskirovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маскировать.html>маскирова́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">замаскиро́вывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mask, to disguise</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to camouflage</li></ol>

***замахавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замахать.html>замаха́вший</a> (8049)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замахать.html>замаха́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamaxávšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замахиваться.html>зама́хиваться</a> (19527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замахнуться.html>замахну́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamaxnútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замахиваться.html>зама́хиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamáxivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замахнуться.html>замахну́ться</a></b>)

***замахнуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замахнуться.html>замахну́ться</a> (11638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замахнуться.html>замахну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamaxnútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замахиваться.html>зама́хиваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to threaten <i>(smb with smth)</i>, to raise <i>(threateningly)</i> <i>(smth at smb)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замахнуться.html>замахну́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamaxnútʹsja</b> na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to raise one's hand against smb</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замахнуться.html>замахну́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:палка.html>па́лкой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamaxnútʹsja</b> pálkoj na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wave/flourish a stick at smb; brandish a stick at smb</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to venture, to make a bold push <i>(for)</i>, to make a stab <i>(at)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">maxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">maxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замахать.html>замаха́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamaxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***замедление.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замедление.html>замедле́ние</a> (20521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>заме́длить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamédlitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замедление.html>замедле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamedlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замедление.html>замедле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замедление.html>замедле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замедление.html>замедле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>slowing down, deceleration; delay</li></ol>

***замедлить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>заме́длить</a> (6278)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медлить.html>ме́длить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">médlitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>заме́длить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamédlitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замедлять.html>замедля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slow down, to decelerate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>заме́длить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:темп.html>те́мпы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamédlitʹ</b> tɛ́mpy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slacken the pace</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>заме́длить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>ход</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamédlitʹ</b> xod</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slow down; reduce speed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>заме́длить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шаги́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamédlitʹ</b> šagí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slow down one's pace; walk slower</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hold back, to delay, to retard</li>
<li><i>in expressions</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>заме́длить</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>zamédlitʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">not to take long <i>(+ to )</i></span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>заме́длил</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:явиться.html>яви́ться</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>zamédlil</b> javítʹsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he did not take long to appear; he was not long in coming</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>заме́длили</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воспользоваться.html>воспо́льзоваться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тим</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní ne <b>zamédlili</b> vospólʹzovatʹsja étim</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they hastened to take advantage of it</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просить.html>прошу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замедлить.html>заме́длить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответ.html>отве́том</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prošú ne <b>zamédlitʹ</b> s otvétom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">please reply immediately [without delay]</span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замедляться.html>замедля́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamedljátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заме́длиться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamédlitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
